L.layerGroup().addTo(map); const rejectedLayer = L.layerGroup().addTo(map); const regionBoundsLayer = L.layerGroup().addTo(map); // 繪製 tiles tiles.forEach(tile => { const bounds = [[tile.bounds[0], tile.bounds[1]], [tile.bounds[2], tile.bounds[3]]]; const color = tile.accepted ? '#4ade80' : '#ff6b6b'; const layer = tile.accepted ? acceptedLayer : rejectedLayer; const rect = L.rectangle(bounds, { color: color, fillColor: color, fillOpacity: 0.4, weight: 1 }); let popup = `${tile.region}

`; popup += `Building Cover: ${tile.cover}%
`; popup += `Jammers: ${tile.num_jammers}
`; popup += `Status: ${tile.accepted ? 'Accepted' : 'Rejected'}
`; if (tile.reject_reason) { popup += `Reason: ${tile.reject_reason}`; } rect.bindPopup(popup); layer.addLayer(rect); }); // 繪製區域邊界 Object.entries(regionBounds).forEach(([name, bounds]) => { const rect = L.rectangle( [[bounds.lat_min, bounds.lon_min], [bounds.lat_max, bounds.lon_max]], { color: '#00d4ff', fillColor: 'transparent', fillOpacity: 0, weight: 3, dashArray: '10, 5' } ); rect.bindPopup(`${name}
Total: ${bounds.total}
Accepted: ${bounds.accepted}`); regionBoundsLayer.addLayer(rect); }); // 生成區域列表 const regionListEl = document.getElementById('region-list'); Object.entries(regionBounds).forEach(([name, bounds]) => { const div = document.createElement('div'); div.className = 'region-item'; div.innerHTML = `
${name}
Total: ${bounds.total} | Accepted: ${bounds.accepted} (${(bounds.accepted/bounds.total*100).toFixed(1)}%)
`; div.onclick = () => { map.fitBounds([[bounds.lat_min, bounds.lon_min], [bounds.lat_max, bounds.lon_max]]); }; regionListEl.appendChild(div); }); // 控制選項 document.getElementById('showAccepted').onchange = function() { if (this.checked) { map.addLayer(acceptedLayer); } else { map.removeLayer(acceptedLayer); } }; document.getElementById('showRejected').onchange = function() { if (this.checked) { map.addLayer(rejectedLayer); } else { map.removeLayer(rejectedLayer); } }; document.getElementById('showRegionBounds').onchange = function() { if (this.checked) { map.addLayer(regionBoundsLayer); } else { map.removeLayer(regionBoundsLayer); } }; // 自動縮放到所有資料範圍 if (tiles.length > 0) { const allBounds = tiles.map(t => [[t.bounds[0], t.bounds[1]], [t.bounds[2], t.bounds[3]]]); const group = L.featureGroup(allBounds.map(b => L.rectangle(b))); map.fitBounds(group.getBounds().pad(0.1)); }
